<h1 _ngcontent-fuy-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="TextArea"> TextArea </h1>

<div _ngcontent-fuy-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;">   <div>    <p>多行文本输入框组件，当输入的文本内容超过组件宽度时会自动换行显示。</p>    <p>高度未设置时，组件无默认高度，自适应内容高度。宽度未设置时，默认撑满最大宽度。</p>    <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">      <p>该组件从API version 7开始支持。后续版本如有新增内容，则采用上角标单独标记该内容的起始版本。</p>     </div></div></div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 182px;">     <h2 id="子组件" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">子组件<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="子组件" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>无</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 429px;">     <h2 id="接口" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">接口<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="接口" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>TextArea(value?: TextAreaOptions)</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" width="25%">TextArea组件参数。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 975px;">     <h2 id="textareaoptions对象说明" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">TextAreaOptions对象说明<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="textareaoptions对象说明" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>TextArea初始化参数。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.5.1.6.1.1" width="20%">名称</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.5.1.6.1.2" width="20%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.5.1.6.1.3" width="20%">只读</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.5.1.6.1.4" width="20%">可选</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.5.1.6.1.5" width="20%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">placeholder</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#resourcestr">ResourceStr</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>设置无输入时的提示文本。输入内容后，提示文本不显示。</p>          <p>仅设置placeholder属性时，手柄依然跟随拖动，手柄松开后光标停留在文字开头位置。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">text</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#resourcestr">ResourceStr</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>设置输入框当前的文本内容。</p>          <p>建议通过onChange事件将状态变量与文本实时绑定，</p>          <p>避免组件刷新时TextArea中的文本内容异常。</p>          <p>从API version 10开始，该参数支持<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-two-way-sync" target="_blank">$$</a>双向绑定变量。</p>          <p>从API version 18开始，该参数支持<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-new-binding#系统组件参数双向绑定" target="_blank">!!</a>双向绑定变量。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">controller<sup>8+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textarea#textareacontroller8">TextAreaController</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">设置TextArea控制器。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 466px;">     <h2 id="属性" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">属性<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="属性" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>除支持<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-component-general-attributes">通用属性</a>，还支持以下属性：</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-size#padding">通用属性padding</a>的默认值为：</p>       <p>{</p>       <p>top: '8vp',</p>       <p>right: '16vp',</p>       <p>bottom: '8vp',</p>       <p>left: '16vp'</p>       <p>}</p>       <p>从API version 11开始，多行输入框可设置.width('auto')使组件宽度自适应文本宽度，自适应时组件宽度受constraintSize属性以及父容器传递的最大最小宽度限制，其余使用方式参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-size">尺寸设置</a>。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 477px;">     <h3 id="placeholdercolor" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">placeholderColor<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 561px;">     <h3 id="placeholderfont" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">placeholderFont<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="placeholderfont" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>placeholderFont(value: Font)</p>     <p>设置placeholder文本样式，包括字体大小、字体粗细、字体族、字体风格。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>可以使用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-graphics-text#loadfontsync">loadFontSync</a>注册自定义字体。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table> width="25%">placeholder文本样式。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 865px;">     <h3 id="textalign" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">textAlign<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="textalign" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>textAlign(value: TextAlign)</p>     <p>设置文本在输入框中的水平对齐方式。</p>     <p>支持TextAlign.Start、TextAlign.Center和TextAlign.End。从API version 11开始，新增TextAlign.JUSTIFY选项。</p>     <p>可通过<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-location#align">align</a>属性控制文本段落在垂直方向上的位置，此组件中不可通过align属性控制文本段落在水平方向上的位置。</p>     <ul>      <li>       <p>Alignment.TopStart、Alignment.Top、Alignment.TopEnd：内容顶部对齐。</p></li>      <li>       <p>Alignment.Start、Alignment.Center、Alignment.End：内容垂直居中。</p></li>      <li>       <p>Alignment.BottomStart、Alignment.Bottom、Alignment.BottomEnd：内容底部对齐。</p></li>     </ul>     <p>当textAlign属性设置为TextAlign.JUSTIFY时，最后一行文本不参与两端对齐，为水平对齐首部效果。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.11.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.11.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.11.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.11.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-appendix-enums#textalign">TextAlign</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>文本在输入框中的水平对齐方式。</p>          <p>默认值：TextAlign.Start</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>textAlign只能调整文本整体的布局，不影响字符的显示顺序。若需要调整字符的显示顺序，请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-internationalization#镜像状态字符对齐" target="_blank">镜像状态字符对齐</a>。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 585px;">     <h3 id="caretcolor" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">caretColor<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead> href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textarea#type11">type</a>接口附带的文本过滤效果失效。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 802px;">     <h3 id="showcounter10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">showCounter<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="showcounter10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>showCounter(value: boolean, options?: InputCounterOptions)</p>     <p>设置当通过InputCounterOptions输入的字符数超过阈值时显示计数器。未调用showCounter接口时，默认不显示计数器。</p>     <p>参数value为true时，才能设置options，文本框开启计数器功能，需要配合maxLength（设置最大字符限制）一起使用。字符计数器显示的效果是当前输入字符数/最大可输入字符数。</p>     <p>当输入字符数大于最大字符数乘百分比值时，显示字符计数器。如果用户设置计数器时不设置InputCounterOptions，那么当前输入字符数达到最大字符数时，边框和计数器下标将变为红色。用户同时设置参数value为true和InputCounterOptions，当thresholdPercentage数值在有效区间内，且输入字符数超过最大字符数时，边框和计数器下标将变为红色，框体抖动。highlightBorder设置为false，则不显示红色边框，计数器默认显示红色边框。内联模式下字符计数器不显示。</p>     <p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textarea#示例2设置计数器">示例2（设置计数器）</a>展示了设置showCounter的效果。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.20.10.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.20.10.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.20.10.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.20.10.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>是否显示计数器。</p>          <p>true表示显示计数器，false表示不显示。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">计数器的配置项。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection"        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.21.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.21.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th> class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 613px;">     <h3 id="enablekeyboardonfocus10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">enableKeyboardOnFocus<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="enablekeyboardonfocus10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>enableKeyboardOnFocus(value: boolean)</p>     <p>设置TextArea通过点击以外的方式获焦时，是否主动拉起软键盘。</p>     <p>从API version 10开始，获焦默认绑定输入法。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 613px;">     <h3 id="minlines20" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">minLines<sup>20+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="minlines20" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>minLines(lines: Optional&lt;number&gt;)</p>     <p>设置最小行数。组件的高度将根据lines自动调整，确保显示高度不低于lines对应的高度。如果设置了<a device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">customKeyboard<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="customkeyboard10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>customKeyboard(value: CustomBuilder, options?: KeyboardOptions)</p>     <p>设置自定义键盘。</p>     <p>当设置自定义键盘时，输入框激活后不会打开系统输入法，而是加载指定的自定义组件。</p>     <p>自定义键盘的高度可以通过自定义组件根节点的height属性设置，宽度则使用系统默认值。</p>     <p>自定义键盘采用覆盖原始界面的方式呈现，当没有开启避让模式或者输入框不需要避让的场景，不会对应用原始界面产生压缩或者上提。</p>     <p>自定义键盘无法获取焦点，但是会拦截手势事件。</p>     <p>默认在输入控件失去焦点时，关闭自定义键盘，开发者也可以通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textarea#textareacontroller8">TextAreaController</a>.<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textarea#stopediting10">stopEditing</a>方法控制键盘关闭。</p>     <p>当设置自定义键盘时，可以通过绑定<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-events-key#onkeypreime12">onKeyPrelme</a>事件规避物理键盘的输入。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>该接口不支持在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-attribute-modifier#attributemodifier">attributeModifier</a>中调用。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.28.14.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.28.14.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" <h3 id="lineheight12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">lineHeight<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>lineHeight(value: number | string | Resource)</p>     <p>设置文本的文本行高，设置值不大于0时，不限制文本行高，自适应字体大小，number类型时单位为fp。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.33.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.33.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.33.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.33.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number | string | <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#resource">Resource</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">文本的文本行高。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>特殊字符字体高度远超出同行的其他字符高度时，文本框出现截断、遮挡、内容相对位置发生变化等不符合预期的显示异常，需要开发者调整组件高度、行高等属性，修改对应的页面布局。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 801px;">     <h3 id="decoration12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">decoration<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="decoration12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>decoration(value: TextDecorationOptions)</p>     <p>设置文本装饰线类型样式及其颜色。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.34.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.34.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.34.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.34.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-text-style#textdecorationoptions12对象说明">TextDecorationOptions</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>文本装饰线对象。</p>          <p>默认值：{</p>          <p>type: TextDecorationType.None,</p>          <p>color: Color.Black,</p>          <p>style: TextDecorationStyle.SOLID</p>          <p>}</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>当文字的下边缘轮廓与装饰线位置相交时，会触发下划线避让规则，下划线将在这些字符处避让文字。常见“gjyqp”等英文字符。</p>       <p>当文本装饰线的颜色设置为Color.Transparent时，装饰线颜色设置为跟随每行第一个字的字体颜色。当文本装饰线的颜色设置为透明色16进制对应值“#00FFFFFF”时，装饰线颜色设置为透明色。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 613px;">     <h3 id="letterspacing12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">letterSpacing<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="letterspacing12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>letterSpacing(value: number | string | Resource)</p>     <p>设置文本字符间距。设置该值为百分比时，按默认值显示。当设置该值为0时，使用默认值。string类型支持number类型取值的字符串形式，可以附带单位，例如"10"、"10fp"。</p>     <p>当取值为负值时，文字会发生压缩，负值过小时会将组件内容区大小压缩为0，导致无内容显示。</p>     <p>对每个字符生效，包括行尾字符。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.35.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.35.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.35.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.35.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number | string | <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#resource">Resource</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>文本字符间距。</p>          <p>单位：<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-pixel-units">fp</a></p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 853px;">     <h3 id="fontfeature12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">fontFeature<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="fontfeature12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>fontFeature(value: string)</p>     <p>设置文字特性效果，比如数字等宽的特性。</p>     <p>格式为：normal | &lt;feature-tag-value&gt;</p>     <p>&lt;feature-tag-value&gt;的格式为：&lt;string&gt; [ &lt;integer&gt; | on | off ]</p>     <p>&lt;feature-tag-value&gt;的个数可以有多个，中间用','隔开。</p>     <p>例如，使用等宽数字的输入格式为："ss01" on。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.36.11.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.36.11.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.36.11.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.36.11.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">文字特性效果。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p>Font Feature当前支持的属性见 <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#fontfeature12">fontFeature属性列表</a>。</p>     <p>设置 Font Feature 属性，Font Feature 是 OpenType 字体的高级排版能力，如支持连字、数字等宽等特性，一般用在自定义字体中，其能力需要字体本身支持。</p>     <p>更多 Font Feature 能力介绍可参考 <a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-fonts-3/#font-feature-settings-prop" target="_blank">https://www.w3.org/TR/css-fonts-3/#font-feature-settings-prop</a> 和 <a href="https://sparanoid.com/lab/opentype-features/" target="_blank">https://sparanoid.com/lab/opentype-features/</a></p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 609px;">     <h3 id="wordbreak12" 777px;">     <h3 id="textoverflow12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">textOverflow<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="textoverflow12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>textOverflow(value: TextOverflow)</p>     <p>设置文本超长时的显示方式。</p>     <p>内联模式，主动配置textOverflow才会生效按<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textarea#maxlines10">maxLines</a>截断效果，不配置时，默认不截断。</p>     <p>文本截断是按字截断。例如，英文以单词为最小单位进行截断，若需要以字母为单位进行截断，<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-appendix-enums#wordbreak11">wordBreak</a>属性可设置为WordBreak.BREAK_ALL。</p>     <p>当textOverflow设置为TextOverflow.None、TextOverflow.Clip、TextOverflow.Ellipsis时，需配合<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textarea#maxlines10">maxLines</a>使用，单独设置不生效。设置TextOverflow.None与TextOverflow.Clip效果一样。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.41.10.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.41.10.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.41.10.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.41.10.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-appendix-enums#textoverflow">TextOverflow</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>文本超长时的显示方式。</p>          <p>默认值：TextOverflow.Clip</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>TextArea组件不支持设置TextOverflow.MARQUEE模式,当设置为TextOverflow.MARQUEE模式时 显示为TextOverflow.Clip</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 637px;">     <h3 id="minfontsize12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">minFontSize<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="minfontsize12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>minFontSize(value: number | string | Resource)</p>     <p>设置文本最小显示字号。string类型支持number类型取值的字符串形式，可以附带单位，例如"10"、"10fp"。</p>     <p>需配合<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textarea#maxfontsize12">maxFontSize</a>以及<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textarea#maxlines10">maxLines</a>或布局大小限制使用，单独设置不生效。</p>     <p>自适应字号生效时，fontSize设置不生效。</p>     <p>minFontSize小于或等于0时，自适应字号不生效，此时按照<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textarea#fontsize">fontSize</a>属性的值生效，未设置时按照其默认值生效。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number | string | <a </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 661px;">     <h3 id="maxfontsize12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">maxFontSize<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="maxfontsize12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>maxFontSize(value: number | string | Resource)</p>     <p>设置文本最大显示字号。string类型支持number类型取值的字符串形式，可以附带单位，例如"10"、"10fp"。</p>     <p>需配合<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textarea#minfontsize12">minFontSize</a>以及<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textarea#maxlines10">maxLines</a>或布局大小限制使用，单独设置不生效。</p>     <p>自适应字号生效时，fontSize设置不生效。</p>     <p>maxFontSize小于等于0或者maxFontSize小于minFontSize时，自适应字号不生效，此时按照<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textarea#fontsize">fontSize</a>属性的值生效，未设置时按照其默认值生效。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">   <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>文本最大显示字号。</p>          <p>单位：<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-pixel-units">fp</a></p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 805px;">     <h3 id="heightadaptivepolicy12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">heightAdaptivePolicy<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="heightadaptivepolicy12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>heightAdaptivePolicy(value: TextHeightAdaptivePolicy)</p>     <p>设置文本自适应高度的方式。</p>     <p>当设置为TextHeightAdaptivePolicy.MAX_LINES_FIRST时，优先使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textarea#maxlines10">maxLines</a>属性来调整文本高度。如果使用maxLines属性的布局大小超过了布局约束，则尝试在<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textarea#minfontsize12">minFontSize</a>和<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textarea#maxfontsize12">maxFontSize</a>的范围内缩小字体以显示更多文本。</p>     <p>组件设置为内联输入风格，编辑态与非编辑态存在字体大小不一致情况。</p>     <p>当设置为TextHeightAdaptivePolicy.MIN_FONT_SIZE_FIRST时，优先使用minFontSize属性来调整文本高度。如果使用minFontSize属性可以将文本布局在一行中，则尝试在minFontSize和maxFontSize的范围内增大字体并使用最大可能的字体大小。</p>     <p>当设置为TextHeightAdaptivePolicy.LAYOUT_CONSTRAINT_FIRST时，优先使用布局约束来调整文本高度。如果布局大小超过布局约束，则尝试在minFontSize和maxFontSize的范围内缩小字体以满足布局约束。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.44.11.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.44.11.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.44.11.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.44.11.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-appendix-enums#textheightadaptivepolicy10">TextHeightAdaptivePolicy</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>文本自适应高度的方式。</p>          <p>默认值：TextHeightAdaptivePolicy.MAX_LINES_FIRST</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 469px;">     <h3 id="linespacing12" id="enablepreviewtext12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">enablePreviewText<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>enablePreviewText(enable: boolean)</p>     <p>设置是否开启输入预上屏。</p>     <p>预上屏内容定义为文字暂存态，目前不支持文字拦截功能。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.49.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.49.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>   </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">enable</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>“预上屏”描述的是一种文字暂存状态。需要在输入法中开启预上屏功能，在输入文本过程中，未确认输入候选词时，文本框中显示标记文本。例如，通过拼音输入中文时，未确定候选词之前，在输入框中显示拼音字母，该状态称为文字预上屏。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" <p>onWillChange的回调时序晚于onWillInsert、onWillDelete，早于onDidInsert、onDidDelete。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 15开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.75.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.75.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.75.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.75.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">callback</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Callback&lt;<a width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>在文本内容将要发生变化时的回调。</p>          <p>返回true时，表示正常修改。返回false时，表示拦截此次触发。</p></td>        </tr>
